States state symbols">\n          Lists of United States state symbols\n         </a>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        Maryland\n       </b>\n       (\n       <span class="nowrap">\n        <span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt">\n         <a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">\n          /\n          <span style="border-bottom:1px dotted">\n           <span title="/\xcb\x88/: primary stress follows">\n            \xcb\x88\n           </span>\n           <span title="\'m\' in \'my\'">\n            m\n           </span>\n           <span title="/\xc9\x9br/: \'err\' in \'merry\'">\n            \xc9\x9br\n           </span>\n           <span title="/\xc9\xaa/: \'i\' in \'kit\'">\n            \xc9\xaa\n           </span>\n           <span title="\'l\' in \'lie\'">\n            l\n           </span>\n           <span title="/\xc9\x99/: \'a\' in \'about\'">\n            \xc9\x99\n           </span>\n           <span title="\'n\' in \'nigh\'">\n            n\n           </span>\n           <span title="\'d\' in \'dye\'">\n            d\n           </span>\n          </span>\n          /\n         </a>\n        </span>\n        <small class="nowrap">\n         (\n         <span class="unicode haudio">\n          <span class="fn">\n           <span style="white-space:nowrap">\n            <a href="/wiki/File:En-us-Maryland.ogg" title="About this sound">\n             <img alt="About this sound" data-file-height="20" data-file-width="20" height="11" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" width="11"/>\n            </a>\n           </span>\n           <a class="internal" href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/1/1f/En-us-Maryland.ogg" title="En-us-Maryland.ogg">\n            listen\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </span>\n         )\n        </small>\n       </span>\n       )\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9">\n        <a href="#cite_note-9">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       is a\n       <a href="/wiki/U.S._state" title="U.S. state">\n        state\n       </a>\n       in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mid-Atlantic_states" title="Mid-Atlantic states">\n        Mid-Atlantic\n       </a>\n       region of the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">\n        United States\n       </a>\n       , bordering\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">\n        Virginia\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/West_Virginia" title="West Virginia">\n        West Virginia\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">\n        Washington, D.C.\n       </a>\n       to its south and west;\n       <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">\n        Pennsylvania\n       </a>\n       to its north; and\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware" title="Delaware">\n        Delaware\n       </a>\n       to its east. The state\'s largest city is\n       <a href="/wiki/Baltimore" title="Baltimore">\n        Baltimore\n       </a>\n       , and its capital is\n       <a href="/wiki/Annapolis,_Maryland" title="Annapolis, Maryland">\n        Annapolis\n       </a>\n       . Among its occasional nicknames are\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Maryland_400" title="Maryland 400">\n         Old Line State\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       , the\n       <i>\n        Free State\n       </i>\n       , and the\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay" title="Chesapeake Bay">\n         Chesapeake Bay\n        </a>\n        State\n       </i>\n       . The state is named after the English queen\n       <a href="/wiki/Henrietta_Maria_of_France" title="Henrietta Maria of France">\n        Henrietta Maria of France\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-10">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       One of the original\n       <a href="/wiki/Thirteen_Colonies" title="Thirteen Colonies">\n        Thirteen Colonies\n       </a>\n       , Maryland is considered to be the birthplace of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Religious_freedom" title="Religious freedom">\n        religious freedom\n       </a>\n       in America,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cecilius_Calvert_2010_11-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Cecilius_Calvert_2010-11">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stmaryscity.org_12-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stmaryscity.org-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       when it was formed by\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/George_Calvert" title="George Calvert">\n        George Calvert\n       </a>\n       in the early 17th century as an intended refuge for persecuted Catholics from England.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cecilius_Calvert_2010_11-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Cecilius_Calvert_2010-11">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stmaryscity.org_12-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stmaryscity.org-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">\n        <a href="#cite_note-13">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       George Calvert was the first Lord of Baltimore and the first English proprietor of the then-Maryland colonial grant.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cecilius_Calvert_2010_11-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Cecilius_Calvert_2010-11">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stmaryscity.org_12-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-stmaryscity.org-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maryland was the seventh state to ratify the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Constitution" title="United States Constitution">\n        United States Constitution\n       </a>\n       , and played a pivotal role in the founding of Washington, D.C., which was established on land donated by the state.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Maryland is\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_U.S._states_and_territories_by_area" title="List of U.S. states and territories by area">\n        one of the smallest U.S. states\n       </a>\n       in terms of area, as well as one of the\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_U.S._states_by_population_density" title="List of U.S. states by population density">\n        most densely populated\n       </a>\n       , with around six million residents. As of 2009\n       <sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;">\n        <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Maryland&amp;action=edit">\n         [update]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       , Maryland had the\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_U.S._states_by_income" title="List of U.S. states by income">\n        highest median household income\n       </a>\n       of any state, owing in large part to its close proximity to the nation\'s capital and a highly diversified economy spanning manufacturing, services, and biotechnology.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14">\n        <a href="#cite_note-14">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toc" id="toc">\n         </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-46">\n           <a href="#Public_libraries">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             8.3\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Public libraries\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-51">\n         <a href="#External_links">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           13\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           External links\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">\n        Geography\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Geography">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_islands_of_Maryland" title="List of islands of Maryland">\n        List of islands of Maryland\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_rivers_of_Maryland" title="List of rivers of Maryland">\n        List of rivers of Maryland\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Maryland has an area of 12,406.68 square miles (32,133.2\xc2\xa0km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ) and is comparable in overall area with\n       <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">\n        Belgium\n       </a>\n       (11,787 square miles (30,530\xc2\xa0km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       )).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">\n        <a href="#cite_note-15">\n         [15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It is the 42nd largest and 9th smallest state and is closest in size to the state of\n       <a href="/wiki/Hawaii" title="Hawaii">\n        Hawaii\n       </a>\n       (10,930.98 square miles (28,311.1\xc2\xa0km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       )), the next smallest state. The next largest state, its neighbor\n       <a href="/wiki/West_Virginia" title="West Virginia">\n        West Virginia\n       </a>\n       , is almost twice the size of Maryland (24,229.76 square miles (62,754.8\xc2\xa0km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       )).\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:452px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:MDGeoReg.PNG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="492" data-file-width="751" height="295" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/1/1e/MDGeoReg.PNG 2x" width="450"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:MDGeoReg.PNG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Physical regions of Maryland\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Description">\n        Description\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Description">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <div          </a>\n           by\n           <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">\n            adding citations Unsourced material may be challenged and\n           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">\n            removed\n           </a>\n           .\n          </span>\n          <small>\n           <i>\n            (April 2017)\n           </i>\n          </small>\n          <small class="hide-when-compact">\n           <i>\n            (\n            <a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">\n             Learn how and when to remove this template message\n            </a>\n            )\n           </i>\n          </small>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Maryland possesses a variety of\n       <a href="/wiki/Topography" title="Topography">\n        topography\n       </a>\n       within its borders, contributing to its nickname\n       <i>\n        America in Miniature\n       </i>\n       . It ranges from sandy\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dunes" title="Dunes">\n        dunes\n       </a>\n       dotted with seagrass in the east, to low marshlands teeming with wildlife and large\n       <a href="/wiki/Taxodium" title="Taxodium">\n        bald cypress\n       </a>\n       near the Chesapeake Bay, to gently rolling hills of oak forests in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Piedmont_(United_States)" title="Piedmont (United States)">\n        Piedmont Region\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Pine" title="Pine">\n        pine\n       </a>\n       groves in the\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_mountains_in_Maryland" title="List of mountains in Maryland">\n        Maryland mountains\n       </a>\n       to the west.\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Deep_Creek_Lake_Maryland_Panoramic_View.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="143" data-file-width="303" height="118" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Deep_Creek_Lake_Maryland_Panoramic_View.jpg/250px-Deep_Creek_Lake_Maryland_Panoramic_View.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/1/18/Deep_Creek_Lake_Maryland_Panoramic_View.jpg 1.5x" width="250"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Deep_Creek_Lake_Maryland_Panoramic_View.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Western Maryland: known for its heavily forested mountains. A panoramic view of\n         <a href="/wiki/Deep_Creek_Lake" title="Deep Creek Lake">\n          Deep Creek Lake\n         </a>\n         and the surrounding\n         <a href="/wiki/Appalachian_Mountains" title="Appalachian Mountains">\n          Appalachian Mountains\n         </a>\n         in\n         <a href="/wiki/Garrett_County,_Maryland" title="Garrett County, Maryland">\n          Garrett County\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Great_Falls,_Maryland,_cliffs.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3008" height="166" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Great_Falls%2C_Maryland%2C_cliffs.jpg/250px-Great_Falls%2C_Maryland%2C_cliffs.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Great_Falls%2C_Maryland%2C_cliffs.jpg/375px-Great_Falls%2C_Maryland%2C_cliffs.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Great_Falls%2C_Maryland%2C_cliffs.jpg/500px-Great_Falls%2C_Maryland%2C_cliffs.jpg 2x" width="250"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Great_Falls,_Maryland,_cliffs.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Great_Falls_(Potomac_River)" title="Great Falls (Potomac River)">\n          Great Falls\n         </a>\n         on the\n         <a href="/wiki/Potomac_River" title="Potomac River">\n          Potomac River\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Maryland is bounded on its north by\n       <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">\n        Pennsylvania\n       </a>\n       , on its west by\n       <a href="/wiki/West_Virginia" title="West Virginia">\n        West Virginia\n       </a>\n       , on its east by\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware" title="Delaware">\n        Delaware\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">\n        Atlantic Ocean\n       </a>\n       , and on its south, across the\n       <a href="/wiki/Potomac_River" title="Potomac River">\n        Potomac River\n       </a>\n       , by West Virginia and\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">\n        Virginia\n       </a>\n       . The mid-portion of this border is interrupted by\n       <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">\n        Washington, D.C.\n       </a>\n       , which sits on land that was originally part of\n       <a href="/wiki/Montgomery_County,_Maryland" title="Montgomery County, Maryland">\n        Montgomery\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Prince_George%27s_County,_Maryland" title="Prince George\'s County, Maryland">\n        Prince George\'s\n       </a>\n       counties and including the town of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Georgetown,_D.C." title="Georgetown, D.C.">\n        Georgetown, Maryland\n       </a>\n       . This land was ceded to the United States Federal Government in 1790 to form the\n       <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">\n        District of Columbia\n       </a>\n       . (The\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">\n        Commonwealth of Virginia\n       </a>\n       gave land south of the Potomac, including the town of\n       <a href="/wiki/Alexandria,_Virginia" title="Alexandria, Virginia">\n        Alexandria, Virginia\n       </a>\n       , however Virginia retroceded its portion in 1846). The\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay" title="Chesapeake Bay">\n        Chesapeake Bay\n       </a>\n       nearly bisects the state and the counties east of the bay are known collectively as the\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Shore_of_Maryland" title="Eastern Shore of Maryland">\n         Eastern Shore\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Patapsco_fg01.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="750" data-file-width="1000" height="188" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Patapsco_fg01.jpg/250px-Patapsco_fg01.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Patapsco_fg01.jpg/375px-Patapsco_fg01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Patapsco_fg01.jpg/500px-Patapsco_fg01.jpg 2x" width="250"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Patapsco_fg01.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Typical freshwater river above the tidal zone. The\n         <a href="/wiki/Patapsco_River" title="Patapsco River">\n          Patapsco River\n         </a>\n         includes the famous\n         <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Viaduct" title="Thomas Viaduct">\n          Thomas Viaduct\n         </a>\n         and is part of the\n         <a href="/wiki/Patapsco_Valley_State_Park" title="Patapsco Valley State Park">\n          Patapsco Valley State Park\n         </a>\n         . Later, the river forms the\n         <a href="/wiki/Inner_Harbor" title="Inner Harbor">\n          Inner Harbor\n         </a>\n         as it empties into the\n         <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay" title="Chesapeake Bay">\n          Chesapeake Bay\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sunset_over_the_marsh_at_Cardinal_Cove_-_NOAA.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1192" data-file-width="1840" height="162" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Sunset_over_the_marsh_at_Cardinal_Cove_-_NOAA.jpg/250px-Sunset_over_the_marsh_at_Cardinal_Cove_-_NOAA.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Sunset_over_the_marsh_at_Cardinal_Cove_-_NOAA.jpg/375px-Sunset_over_the_marsh_at_Cardinal_Cove_-_NOAA.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Sunset_over_the_marsh_at_Cardinal_Cove_-_NOAA.jpg/500px-Sunset_over_the_marsh_at_Cardinal_Cove_-_NOAA.jpg 2x" width="250"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sunset_over_the_marsh_at_Cardinal_Cove_-_NOAA.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Typical brackish tidal river. Sunset over a marsh at Cardinal Cove on the\n         <a href="/wiki/Patuxent_River" title="Patuxent River">\n          Patuxent River\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ChesapeakeTidalWetlands.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1704" data-file-width="2272" height="188" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/ChesapeakeTidalWetlands.jpg/250px-ChesapeakeTidalWetlands.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/ChesapeakeTidalWetlands.jpg/375px-ChesapeakeTidalWetlands.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/ChesapeakeTidalWetlands.jpg/500px-ChesapeakeTidalWetlands.jpg 2x" width="250"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:ChesapeakeTidalWetlands.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Tidal wetlands of the\n         <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay" title="Chesapeake Bay">\n          Chesapeake Bay\n         </a>\n         , the largest\n         <a href="/wiki/Estuary" title="Estuary">\n          estuary\n         </a>\n         in the United States and the largest water feature in Maryland.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Most of the state\'s waterways are part of the Chesapeake Bay watershed, with the exceptions of a tiny portion of extreme western\n       <a href="/wiki/Garrett_County,_Maryland" title="Garrett County, Maryland">\n        Garrett County\n       </a>\n       (drained by the\n       <a href="/wiki/Youghiogheny_River" title="Youghiogheny River">\n        Youghiogheny River\n       </a>\n       as part of the watershed of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mississippi_River" title="Mississippi River">\n        Mississippi River\n       </a>\n       ), the eastern half of Worcester County (which drains into Maryland\'s Atlantic coastal bays), and a small portion of the state\'s northeast corner (which drains into the\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_River" title="Delaware River">\n        Delaware River\n       </a>\n       watershed). So prominent is the Chesapeake in Maryland\'s geography and economic life that there has been periodic agitation to change the state\'s official nickname to the "Bay State", a nickname that has been used by\n       <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts" title="Massachusetts">\n        Massachusetts\n       </a>\n       for decades.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The highest point in Maryland, with an elevation of 3,360 feet (1,020\xc2\xa0m), is\n       <a href="/wiki/Backbone_Mountain" title="Backbone Mountain">\n        Hoye Crest on Backbone Mountain\n       </a>\n       , in the southwest corner of\n       <a href="/wiki/Garrett_County,_Maryland" title="Garrett County, Maryland">\n        Garrett County\n       </a>\n       , near the border with West Virginia, and near the headwaters of the North Branch of the Potomac River. Close to the small town of\n       <a href="/wiki/Hancock,_Maryland" title="Hancock, Maryland">\n        Hancock\n       </a>\n       , in western Maryland, about two-thirds of the way across the state, there are 1.83 miles (2.95\xc2\xa0km) between its borders. This geographical curiosity makes Maryland the narrowest state,\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2012)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       bordered by the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mason%E2%80%93Dixon_line" title="Mason\xe2\x80\x93Dixon line">\n        Mason\xe2\x80\x93Dixon line\n       </a>\n       to the north, and the northwards-arching\n       <a href="/wiki/Potomac_River" title="Potomac River">\n        Potomac River\n       </a>\n       to the south.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Portions of Maryland are included in various official and unofficial geographic regions. For example, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Delmarva_Peninsula" title="Delmarva Peninsula">\n        Delmarva Peninsula\n       </a>\n       is composed of the Eastern Shore counties of Maryland, the entire\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/State_of_Delaware" title="State of Delaware">\n        state of Delaware\n       </a>\n       , and the two counties that make up the\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Shore_of_Virginia" title="Eastern Shore of Virginia">\n        Eastern Shore of Virginia\n       </a>\n       , whereas the westernmost counties of Maryland are considered part of\n       <a href="/wiki/Appalachia" title="Appalachia">\n        Appalachia\n       </a>\n       . Much of the Baltimore\xe2\x80\x93Washington corridor lies just south of the Piedmont in the Coastal Plain,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">\n        <a href="#cite_note-16">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       though it straddles the border between the two regions.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Geology">\n        Geology\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Geology">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Earthquakes in Maryland are infrequent and small due to the state\'s distance from seismic/earthquake zones.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17">\n        <a href="#cite_note-17">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">\n        <a href="#cite_note-18">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Moment_magnitude_scale" title="Moment magnitude scale">\n        M\n       </a>\n       5.8\n       <a href="/wiki/2011_Virginia_earthquake" title="2011 Virginia earthquake">\n        Virginia earthquake in 2011\n       </a>\n       was felt moderately throughout Maryland. Buildings in the state are not well-designed for earthquakes and can suffer damage easily.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2012)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The lack of any glacial history accounts for the scarcity of Maryland\'s natural lakes, yet the oft-repeated claim\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19">\n        <a href="#cite_note-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       that Maryland is the only state without natural lakes is not true. Laurel Oxbow Lake is an over one-hundred-year-old 55-acre natural lake two miles north of\n       <a href="/wiki/Maryland_City,_Maryland" title="Maryland City, Maryland">\n        Maryland City\n       </a>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">\n        <a href="#cite_note-20">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">\n        <a href="#cite_note-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">\n        <a href="#cite_note-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and adjacent to\n       <a href="/wiki/Russett,_Maryland" title="Russett, Maryland">\n        Russett\n       </a>\n       . "Chews Lake" is a seven-acre natural lake two miles south-southeast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Upper_Marlboro,_Maryland" title="Upper Marlboro, Maryland">\n        Upper Marlboro\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">\n        <a href="#cite_note-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There are numerous man-made lakes, the largest of them being the\n       <a href="/wiki/Deep_Creek_Lake" title="Deep Creek Lake">\n        Deep Creek Lake\n       </a>\n       , a reservoir in\n       <a href="/wiki/Garrett_County,_Maryland" title="Garrett County, Maryland">\n        Garrett County\n       </a>\n       in westernmost Maryland.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Maryland has shale formations containing natural gas, where fracking is theoretically possible.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-natgas_24-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-natgas-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Flora">\n        Flora\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Flora">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:BESusan.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="960" data-file-width="1280" height="188" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/BESusan.JPG/250px-BESusan.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/BESusan.JPG/375px-BESusan.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/BESusan.JPG/500px-BESusan.JPG 2x" width="250"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:BESusan.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Rudbeckia_hirta" title="Rudbeckia hirta">\n          Black-eyed susans\n         </a>\n         , the state flower, grow throughout much of the state.\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-maag-flower_25-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-maag-flower-25">\n           [25]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       As is typical of states on the\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States" title="East Coast of the United States">\n        East Coast\n       </a>\n       , Maryland\'s plant life is abundant and healthy. A good dose of annual precipitation helps to support many types of plants, including\n       <a href="/wiki/Seagrass" title="Seagrass">\n        seagrass\n       </a>\n       and various\n       <a href="/wiki/Phragmites" title="Phragmites">\n        reeds\n       </a>\n       at the smaller end of the spectrum to the gigantic\n       <a href="/wiki/Wye_Oak" title="Wye Oak">\n        Wye Oak\n       </a>\n       , a huge example of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/White_oak" title="White oak">\n        white oak\n       </a>\n       , the state tree, which can grow in excess of 70 feet (21\xc2\xa0m) tall.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Middle_Atlantic_coastal_forests" title="Middle Atlantic coastal forests">\n        Middle Atlantic coastal forests\n       </a>\n       , typical of the southeastern\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_coastal_plain" title="Atlantic coastal plain">\n        Atlantic coastal plain\n       </a>\n       , grow around Chesapeake Bay and on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Delmarva_Peninsula" title="Delmarva Peninsula">\n        Delmarva Peninsula\n       </a>\n       . Moving west, a mixture of\n       <a href="/wiki/Northeastern_coastal_forests" title="Northeastern coastal forests">\n        Northeastern coastal forests\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Southeastern_mixed_forests" title="Southeastern mixed forests">\n        Southeastern mixed forests\n       </a>\n       cover the central part of the state. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Appalachian_Mountains" title="Appalachian Mountains">\n        Appalachian Mountains\n       </a>\n       of western Maryland are home to\n       <a href="/wiki/Appalachian-Blue_Ridge_forests" title="Appalachian-Blue Ridge forests">\n        Appalachian-Blue Ridge forests\n       </a>\n       . These give way to\n       <a href="/wiki/Appalachian_mixed_mesophytic_forests" title="Appalachian mixed mesophytic forests">\n        Appalachian mixed mesophytic forests\n       </a>\n       near the West Virginia border.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ecoregions_26-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ecoregions-26">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Palmtree_solomons.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="400" data-file-width="256" height="344" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Palmtree_solomons.jpg/220px-Palmtree_solomons.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/d/d1/Palmtree_solomons.jpg 1.5x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Palmtree_solomons.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Mature\n         <i>\n          Trachycarpus fortunei\n         </i>\n         in\n         <a href="/wiki/Solomons,_Maryland" title="Solomons, Maryland">\n          Solomons, Maryland\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Many foreign species are cultivated in the state, some as ornamentals, others as novelty species. Included among these are the\n       <a href="/wiki/Lagerstroemia" title="Lagerstroemia">\n        crape myrtle\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Italian_cypress" title="Italian cypress">\n        Italian cypress\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Magnolia_grandiflora" title="Magnolia grandiflora">\n        southern magnolia\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Live_oak" title="Live oak">\n        live oak\n       </a>\n       in the warmer parts of the state,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">\n        <a href="#cite_note-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and even\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hardy_palms" title="Hardy palms">\n        hardy palm trees\n       </a>\n       in the warmer central and eastern parts of the state.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">\n        <a href="#cite_note-28">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       USDA plant\n       <a href="/wiki/Hardiness_zone" title="Hardiness zone">\n        hardiness zones\n       </a>\n       in the state range from Zones 5 and 6 in the extreme western part of the state to Zone 7 in the central part, and Zone 8 around the southern part of the coast, the bay area, and parts of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Baltimore_Metropolitan_Area" title="Baltimore Metropolitan Area">\n        metropolitan Baltimore\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arbor_Day_Foundation_29-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Arbor_Day_Foundation-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Invasive plant species, such as\n       <a href="/wiki/Kudzu" title="Kudzu">\n        kudzu\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tree_of_heaven" title="Tree of heaven">\n        tree of heaven\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Multiflora_rose" title="Multiflora rose">\n        multiflora rose\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Microstegium_vimineum" title="Microstegium vimineum">\n        Japanese stiltgrass\n       </a>\n       , stifle growth of endemic plant life.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">\n        <a href="#cite_note-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maryland\'s state flower, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Rudbeckia_hirta" title="Rudbeckia hirta">\n        black-eyed susan\n       </a>\n       , grows in abundance in wild flower groups throughout the state. The state insect, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Baltimore_checkerspot" title="Baltimore checkerspot">\n        Baltimore checkerspot butterfly\n       </a>\n       , is not common as it is near the southern edge of its range.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">\n        <a href="#cite_note-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_Maryland_birds" title="List of Maryland birds">\n        435 species of birds\n       </a>\n       have been reported from Maryland.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MRC_32-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MRC-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Fauna">\n        Fauna\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Fauna">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The state harbors a great number of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/White_tailed_deer" title="White tailed deer">\n        white tailed deer\n       </a>\n       , especially in the woody and mountainous west of the state, and overpopulation can become a problem from year to year. Mammals can be found ranging from the mountains in the west to the central areas and include\n       <a href="/wiki/American_black_bear" title="American black bear">\n        black bears\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Maryland_Wildlife_33-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Maryland_Wildlife-33">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Bobcat" title="Bobcat">\n        bobcats\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34">\n        <a href="#cite_note-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       foxes,\n       <a href="/wiki/Coyote" title="Coyote">\n        coyotes\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">\n        <a href="#cite_note-35">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       raccoons, and otters.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Maryland_Wildlife_33-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Maryland_Wildlife-33">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Assateague_Island_horses_August_2009_4.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="166" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Assateague_Island_horses_August_2009_4.jpg/250px-Assateague_Island_horses_August_2009_4.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Assateague_Island_horses_August_2009_4.jpg/375px-Assateague_Island_horses_August_2009_4.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Assateague_Island_horses_August_2009_4.jpg/500px-Assateague_Island_horses_August_2009_4.jpg 2x" width="250"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Assateague_Island_horses_August_2009_4.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         On Maryland\'s Atlantic coastal islands: A feral\n         <a href="/wiki/Chincoteague_Pony" title="Chincoteague Pony">\n          Chincoteague Pony\n         </a>\n         on\n         <a href="/wiki/Assateague_Island" title="Assateague Island">\n          Assateague\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       There is a population of rare wild (feral) horses found on\n       <a href="/wiki/Assateague_Island" title="Assateague Island">\n        Assateague Island\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-horse_36-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-horse-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       They are believed to be descended from horses who escaped from shipwrecks.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-horse_36-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-horse-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Every year during the last week of July, they are captured and waded across a shallow bay for sale at\n       <a href="/wiki/Chincoteague,_Virginia" title="Chincoteague, Virginia">\n        Chincoteague, Virginia\n       </a>\n       , a conservation technique which ensures the tiny island is not overrun by the horses.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-horse_36-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-horse-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The ponies and their sale were popularized by the children\'s book,\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Misty_of_Chincoteague" title="Misty of Chincoteague">\n         Misty of Chincoteague\n        </a>\n        .\n       </i>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The purebred\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay_Retriever" title="Chesapeake Bay Retriever">\n        Chesapeake Bay Retriever\n       </a>\n       dog was bred specifically for water sports, hunting and search and rescue in the Chesapeake area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Maryland1_37-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Maryland1-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In 1878 the Chesapeake Bay Retriever was the first individual retriever breed recognized by the\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Kennel_Club" title="American Kennel Club">\n        American Kennel Club\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Maryland1_37-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Maryland1-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and was later adopted by the\n       <a href="/wiki/University_of_Maryland,_Baltimore_County" title="University of Maryland, Baltimore County">\n        University of Maryland, Baltimore County\n       </a>\n       as their mascot.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Maryland\'s reptile and amphibian population includes the\n       <a href="/wiki/Diamondback_terrapin" title="Diamondback terrapin">\n        diamondback terrapin\n       </a>\n       turtle, which was adopted as the mascot of\n       <a href="/wiki/University_of_Maryland,_College_Park" title="University of Maryland, College Park">\n        University of Maryland, College Park\n       </a>\n       . The state is part of the territory of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Baltimore_oriole" title="Baltimore oriole">\n        Baltimore oriole\n       </a>\n       , which is the official state bird and mascot of the MLB team the\n       <a href="/wiki/Baltimore_Orioles" title="Baltimore Orioles">\n        Baltimore Orioles\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">\n        <a href="#cite_note-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Environment">\n        Environment\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Environment">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Maryland joined with neighboring states during the end of the 20th century to improve the health of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay" title="Chesapeake Bay">\n        Chesapeake Bay\n       </a>\n       . The bay\'s aquatic life and seafood industry have been threatened by development and by fertilizer and livestock waste entering the bay.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">\n        <a href="#cite_note-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-hog_40-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-hog-40">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In 2007, Forbes.com rated Maryland as the fifth "Greenest" state in the country behind three of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Pacific_States" title="Pacific States">\n        Pacific States\n       </a>\n       and Vermont. Maryland ranks 40th in total energy consumption nationwide, and it managed less toxic waste per capita than all but six states in 2005.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">\n        <a href="#cite_note-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In April 2007 Maryland joined the\n       <a href="/wiki/Regional_Greenhouse_Gas_Initiative" title="Regional Greenhouse Gas Initiative">\n        Regional Greenhouse Gas Initiative\n       </a>\n       (RGGI)\xe2\x80\x94a regional initiative formed by all of the Northeastern states, Washington D.C., and three Canadian provinces to reduce greenhouse gas emissions.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2017)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       In March 2017, Maryland became the first state with proven gas reserves to ban fracking by passing a law against it. Vermont has such a law, but no shale gas, and New York has such a ban, though it was made by executive order.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-natgas_24-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-natgas-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Climate">\n        Climate\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Climate">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:MD_koppen.svg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1116" data-file-width="1440" height="171" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/MD_koppen.svg/220px-MD_koppen.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/MD_koppen.svg/330px-MD_koppen.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/MD_koppen.svg/440px-MD_koppen.svg.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:MD_koppen.svg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A map of K\xc3\xb6ppen climate types in Maryland\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Baltimore_Snowpocalypse.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="685" data-file-width="1024" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Baltimore_Snowpocalypse.jpg/220px-Baltimore_Snowpocalypse.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Baltimore_Snowpocalypse.jpg/330px-Baltimore_Snowpocalypse.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Baltimore_Snowpocalypse.jpg/440px-Baltimore_Snowpocalypse.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Baltimore_Snowpocalypse.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Winter in Baltimore, Lancaster Street, Fells Point\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Maryland has a wide array of climates, due to local variances in elevation, proximity to water, and protection from colder weather due to\n       <a href="/wiki/Katabatic_wind" title="Katabatic wind">\n        downslope winds\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The eastern half of Maryland\xe2\x80\x94which includes the cities of\n       <a href="/wiki/Ocean_City,_Maryland" title="Ocean City, Maryland">\n        Ocean City\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Salisbury,_Maryland" title="Salisbury, Maryland">\n        Salisbury\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Annapolis" title="Annapolis">\n        Annapolis\n       </a>\n       , and the southern and eastern suburbs of Washington, D.C. and\n       <a href="/wiki/Baltimore" title="Baltimore">\n        Baltimore\n       </a>\n       \xe2\x80\x94lies on the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Atlantic_Coastal_Plain" title="Atlantic Coastal Plain">\n        Atlantic Coastal Plain\n       </a>\n       , with flat topography and sandy or muddy soil. This region has a\n       <a href="/wiki/Humid_subtropical_climate" title="Humid subtropical climate">\n        humid subtropical climate\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ppen_climate_classification" title="K\xc3\xb6ppen climate classification">\n        K\xc3\xb6ppen\n       </a>\n       <i>\n        Cfa\n       </i>\n       ), with hot, humid summers and a short, mild to cool winter; it falls under USDA\n       <a href="/wiki/Hardiness_zone" title="Hardiness zone">\n        Hardiness zone\n       </a>\n       8a.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arbor_Day_Foundation_29-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Arbor_Day_Foundation-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Piedmont_(United_States)" title="Piedmont (United States)">\n        Piedmont\n       </a>\n       region\xe2\x80\x94which includes northern and western greater Baltimore,\n       <a href="/wiki/Westminster,_Maryland" title="Westminster, Maryland">\n        Westminster\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Gaithersburg,_Maryland" title="Gaithersburg, Maryland">\n        Gaithersburg\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Frederick,_Maryland" title="Frederick, Maryland">\n        Frederick\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hagerstown,_Maryland" title="Hagerstown, Maryland">\n        Hagerstown\n       </a>\n       \xe2\x80\x94has average seasonal snowfall totals generally exceeding 20 inches (51\xc2\xa0cm) and, as part of USDA Hardiness zones 7b and 7a,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arbor_Day_Foundation_29-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Arbor_Day_Foundation-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       temperatures below 10\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (\xe2\x88\x9212\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) are less rare. From the\n       <a href="/wiki/Cumberland_Valley" title="Cumberland Valley">\n        Cumberland Valley\n       </a>\n       on westward, the climate begins to transition to a\n       <a href="/wiki/Humid_continental_climate" title="Humid continental climate">\n        humid continental climate\n       </a>\n       (K\xc3\xb6ppen\n       <i>\n        Dfa\n       </i>\n       ).\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In western Maryland, the higher elevations of\n       <a href="/wiki/Allegany_County,_Maryland" title="Allegany County, Maryland">\n        Allegany\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Garrett_County,_Maryland" title="Garrett County, Maryland">\n        Garrett\n       </a>\n       counties\xe2\x80\x94including the cities of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cumberland,_Maryland" title="Cumberland, Maryland">\n        Cumberland\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Frostburg,_Maryland" title="Frostburg, Maryland">\n        Frostburg\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Oakland,_Maryland" title="Oakland, Maryland">\n        Oakland\n       </a>\n       \xe2\x80\x94display more characteristics of the humid continental zone, due in part to elevation. They fall under USDA Hardiness zones 6b and below.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arbor_Day_Foundation_29-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Arbor_Day_Foundation-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Precipitation">\n        Precipitation\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Precipitation">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Precipitation in the state is characteristic of the East Coast. Annual rainfall ranges from 35 to 45 inches (890 to 1,140\xc2\xa0mm) with more in higher elevations. Nearly every part of Maryland receives 3.5\xe2\x80\x934.5 inches (89\xe2\x80\x93114\xc2\xa0mm) per month of rain. Average annual snowfall varies from 9 inches (23\xc2\xa0cm) in the coastal areas to over 100 inches (250\xc2\xa0cm) in the western mountains of the state.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n        <a href="#cite_note-42">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricanes_and_tornadoes">\n        Hurricanes and tornadoes\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Hurricanes and tornadoes">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Because of its location near the\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States" title="East Coast of the United States">\n        Atlantic Coast\n       </a>\n       , Maryland is somewhat vulnerable to\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclones" title="Tropical cyclones">\n        tropical cyclones\n       </a>\n       , although the\n       <a href="/wiki/Delmarva_Peninsula" title="Delmarva Peninsula">\n        Delmarva Peninsula\n       </a>\n       and the outer banks of\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">\n        North Carolina\n       </a>\n       provide a large buffer, such that strikes from major hurricanes (category 3 or above) occur infrequently. More often, Maryland gets the remnants of a tropical system which has already come ashore and released most of its energy. Maryland averages around 30\xe2\x80\x9340 days of thunderstorms a year, and averages around six tornado strikes annually.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Annual_average_number_of_tornadoes_43-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Annual_average_number_of_tornadoes-43">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table (14\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C)\n         </small>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <small>\n          78\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (26\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C)\n          <br/>\n          56\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (\xe2\x88\x926\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C)\n         </small>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         <small>\n          <a href="/wiki/Cumberland,_Maryland" title="Cumberland, Maryland">\n           Cumberland\n          </a>\n         </small>\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <small>\n          41\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (5\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C)\n          <br/>\n          22\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (\xe2\x88\x926\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C)\n         </small>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <small>\n          46\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (8\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C)\n          <br/>\n          24\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (\xe2\x88\x924\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C)\n         </small>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <small>\n          56\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (13\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C)\n          <br/>\n
