<td style="padding-left:8px;">\n         3,100,689\n        </td>\n        <td style="font-size:85%">\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px; text-align: center;">\n         32.3%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td style="text-align:center">\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/1970_United_States_Census" title="1970 United States Census">\n           1970\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px;">\n         3,922,399\n        </td>\n        <td style="font-size:85%">\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px; text-align: center;">\n         26.5%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td style="text-align:center">\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/1980_United_States_Census" title="1980 United States Census">\n           1980\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px;">\n         4,216,975\n        </td>\n        <td style="font-size:85%">\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px; text-align: center;">\n         7.5%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td style="text-align:center">\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/1990_United_States_Census" title="1990 United States Census">\n           1990\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px;">\n         4,781,468\n        </td>\n        <td style="font-size:85%">\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px; text-align: center;">\n         13.4%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td style="text-align:center">\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/2000_United_States_Census" title="2000 United States Census">\n           2000\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px;">\n         5,296,486\n        </td>\n        <td style="font-size:85%">\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px; text-align: center;">\n         10.8%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td style="text-align:center">\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/2010_United_States_Census" title="2010 United States Census">\n           2010\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px;">\n         5,773,552\n        </td>\n        <td style="font-size:85%">\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px; text-align: center;">\n         9.0%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td style="text-align:center">\n         <b>\n          Est. 2016\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px;">\n         6,016,447\n        </td>\n        <td style="font-size:85%">\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px; text-align: center;">\n         4.2%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="4" style="border-top:1px solid black; font-size:85%; text-align:center">\n         Source: 1910\xe2\x80\x932010\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91">\n          <a href="#cite_note-91">\n           [91]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         <br/>\n         2015 estimate\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PopEstUS_75-1">\n          <a href="#cite_note-PopEstUS-75">\n           [75]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <table class="wikitable sortable collapsible" style="font-size: 90%;">\n       <caption>\n        <b>\n         Maryland Racial Breakdown of Population\n        </b>\n       </caption>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         Racial composition\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         1970\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-census_92-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-census-92">\n           [92]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         1990\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-census_92-1">\n          <a href="#cite_note-census-92">\n           [92]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         2000\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93">\n          <a href="#cite_note-93">\n           [93]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         2010\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94">\n          <a href="#cite_note-94">\n           [94]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" <td>\n         64.0%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         60.8%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/African_American" title="African American">\n          Black\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         17.8%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         24.9%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         27.9%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         29.8%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Asian_American" title="Asian American">\n          Asian\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.5%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         2.9%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         4.0%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         5.5%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Native_Americans_in_the_United_States" title="Native Americans in the United States">\n          Native\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.1%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.3%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.3%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.3%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Race_and_ethnicity_in_the_United_States_Census" title="Race and ethnicity in the United States Census">\n          Other race\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.1%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.9%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         1.8%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         3.6%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Multiracial_American" title="Multiracial American">\n          Two or more races\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         \xe2\x80\x93\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         \xe2\x80\x93\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         2.0%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         2.9%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Non-Hispanic_whites" title="Non-Hispanic whites">\n          Non-Hispanic whites\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         80.4%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         69.6%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         62.1%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         54.7%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       In 1970 the Census Bureau reported Maryland\'s population as 17.8 percent African-American and 80.4 percent non-Hispanic White.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95">\n        <a href="#cite_note-95">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/African_Americans_in_Maryland" title="African Americans in Maryland">\n        African Americans\n       </a>\n       form a sizable portion of the state\'s population \xe2\x80\x93 nearly 30 percent in 2010.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PopUS_96-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-PopUS-96">\n         [96]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Most are descendants of people transported to the area as slaves from West Africa, and many are of mixed race, including European and Native American ancestry. New residents of African descent include 20th-century and later immigrants from\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nigerian_American" title="Nigerian American">\n        Nigeria\n       </a>\n       , particularly of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Igbo_American" title="Igbo American">\n        Igbo\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Yoruba_people" title="Yoruba people">\n        Yoruba\n       </a>\n       tribes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">\n        <a href="#cite_note-97">\n         [97]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Concentrations of African Americans live in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Baltimore,_Maryland" title="Baltimore, Maryland">\n        Baltimore City\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Prince_George%27s_County,_Maryland" title="Prince George\'s County, Maryland">\n        Prince George\'s County\n       </a>\n       , a suburb of Washington, D.C., where many work;\n       <a href="/wiki/Charles_County,_Maryland" title="Charles County, Maryland">\n        Charles County\n       </a>\n       , western parts of\n       <a href="/wiki/Baltimore_County,_Maryland" title="Baltimore County, Maryland">\n        Baltimore County\n       </a>\n       , and the southern Eastern Shore.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The top reported ancestries by Maryland residents are:\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/German_American" title="German American">\n        German\n       </a>\n       (15%),\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Irish_American" title="Irish American">\n        Irish\n       </a>\n       (11%),\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/English_American" title="English American">\n        English\n       </a>\n       (8%),\n       <a href="/wiki/Americans" title="Americans">\n        American\n       </a>\n       (7%),\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Italian_American" title="Italian American">\n        Italian\n       </a>\n       (6%), and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Polish_American" title="Polish American">\n        Polish\n       </a>\n       (3%).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-98">\n        <a href="#cite_note-98">\n         [98]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Irish_American" title="Irish American">\n        Irish American\n       </a>\n       populations can be found\n       <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Irish_in_Baltimore" title="History of the Irish in Baltimore">\n        throughout the Baltimore area\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-teaching.msa.maryland.gov_99-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-teaching.msa.maryland.gov-99">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and the Northern and Eastern suburbs of Washington D.C. in Maryland (descendents of those who moved out to the suburbs\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-abcswamp_100-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-abcswamp-100">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       of Washington\'s once predominantly Irish neighborhoods\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-abcswamp_100-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-abcswamp-100">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101">\n        <a href="#cite_note-101">\n         [101]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       ), as well as Western Maryland, where Irish immigrant laborers helped to build the C &amp; O Railroad.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-teaching.msa.maryland.gov_99-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-teaching.msa.maryland.gov-99">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Smaller but much older Irish populations can be found in Southern Maryland, with some roots dating as far back as the early Maryland colony.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">\n        <a href="#cite_note-102">\n         [102]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This population, however, still remains culturally very active and yearly festivals are held.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-103">\n        <a href="#cite_note-103">\n         [103]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       A large percentage of the population of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Shore_of_Maryland" title="Eastern Shore of Maryland">\n        Eastern Shore\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Southern_Maryland" title="Southern Maryland">\n        Southern Maryland\n       </a>\n       are descendants of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_American" title="British American">\n        British American\n       </a>\n       ancestry. The Eastern Shore was settled by Protestants, chiefly\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Methodist" title="Methodist">\n        Methodist\n       </a>\n       and the southern counties were initially settled by English Catholics. Western and northern Maryland have large\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/German-American" title="German-American">\n        German-American\n       </a>\n       populations. More recent European immigrants of the late 19th and early 20th century settled first in Baltimore, attracted to its industrial jobs. Many of their ethnic\n       <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Italians_in_Baltimore" title="History of the Italians in Baltimore">\n        Italian\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Poles_in_Baltimore" title="History of the Poles in Baltimore">\n        Polish\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Czechs_in_Baltimore" title="History of the Czechs in Baltimore">\n        Czech\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Lithuanians_in_Baltimore" title="History of the Lithuanians in Baltimore">\n        Lithuanian\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Greeks_in_Baltimore" title="History of the Greeks in Baltimore">\n        Greek\n       </a>\n       descendants still live in the area.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Large\n       <a href="/wiki/Ethnic_groups_in_Baltimore" title="Ethnic groups in Baltimore">\n        ethnic minorities\n       </a>\n       include\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Europe" title="Eastern Europe">\n        Eastern Europeans\n       </a>\n       such as\n       <a href="/wiki/Croatian_Americans" title="Croatian Americans">\n        Croatians\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Belarusian_Americans" title="Belarusian Americans">\n        Belarusians\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Russians_in_Baltimore" title="History of the Russians in Baltimore">\n        Russians\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Ukrainians_in_Baltimore" title="History of the Ukrainians in Baltimore">\n        Ukrainians\n       </a>\n       . The shares of European immigrants born in Eastern Europe increased significantly between 1990 and 2010. Following the dissolution of the Soviet Union, Yugoslavia, and Czechoslovakia, many immigrants from Eastern Europe came to the United States - 12 percent of which currently reside in Maryland.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-104">\n        <a href="#cite_note-104">\n         [104]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105">\n        <a href="#cite_note-105">\n         [105]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Hispanic immigrants of the later 20th century have settled in\n       <a href="/wiki/Aspen_Hill,_Maryland" title="Aspen Hill, Maryland">\n        Aspen Hill\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hyattsville,_Maryland" title="Hyattsville, Maryland">\n        Hyattsville\n       </a>\n       /\n       <a href="/wiki/Langley_Park,_Maryland" title="Langley Park, Maryland">\n        Langley Park\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Glenmont,_Maryland" title="Glenmont, Maryland">\n        Glenmont\n       </a>\n       /\n       <a href="/wiki/Wheaton,_Maryland" title="Wheaton, Maryland">\n        Wheaton\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Bladensburg,_Maryland" title="Bladensburg, Maryland">\n        Bladensburg\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Riverdale_Park,_Maryland" title="Riverdale Park, Maryland">\n        Riverdale Park\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Gaithersburg,_Maryland" title="Gaithersburg, Maryland">\n        Gaithersburg\n       </a>\n       , as well as\n       <a href="/wiki/Highlandtown,_Baltimore" title="Highlandtown, Baltimore">\n        Highlandtown\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Greektown,_Baltimore" title="Greektown, Baltimore">\n        Greektown\n       </a>\n       in East Baltimore.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Salvadoran_American" title="Salvadoran American">\n        Salvadorans\n       </a>\n       are the largest Hispanic group in Maryland. Other Hispanic groups with significant populations in the state include\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mexican_American" title="Mexican American">\n        Mexicans\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Puerto_Rican_American" title="Puerto Rican American">\n        Puerto Ricans\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Honduran_American" title="Honduran American">\n        Hondurans\n       </a>\n       . Though the Salvadoran population is more concentrated in the area around Washington, D.C., and the Puerto Rican population is more concentrated in the Baltimore area, all other major Hispanic groups in the state are evenly dispersed between these two areas. Maryland has one of the most diverse Hispanic populations in the country, with significant populations from various\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spanish_Caribbean" title="Spanish Caribbean">\n        Caribbean\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Central_America" title="Central America">\n        Central American\n       </a>\n       nations.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106">\n        <a href="#cite_note-106">\n         [106]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Jews are numerous throughout\n       <a href="/wiki/Montgomery_County,_Maryland" title="Montgomery County, Maryland">\n        Montgomery County\n       </a>\n       and in\n       <a href="/wiki/Pikesville,_Maryland" title="Pikesville, Maryland">\n        Pikesville\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Owings_Mills" title="Owings Mills">\n        Owings Mills\n       </a>\n       northwest of Baltimore. Asian Americans are concentrated in the suburban counties surrounding Washington, D.C. and in\n       <a href="/wiki/Howard_County,_Maryland" title="Howard County, Maryland">\n        Howard County\n       </a>\n       , with\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Korean_American" title="Korean American">\n        Korean American\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Taiwanese_American" title="Taiwanese American">\n        Taiwanese American\n       </a>\n       communities in\n       <a href="/wiki/Rockville,_Maryland" title="Rockville, Maryland">\n        Rockville\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Gaithersburg,_Maryland" title="Gaithersburg, Maryland">\n        Gaithersburg\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Germantown,_Maryland" title="Germantown, Maryland">\n        Germantown\n       </a>\n       and a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Filipino_American" title="Filipino American">\n        Filipino American\n       </a>\n       community in\n       <a href="/wiki/Fort_Washington,_Maryland" title="Fort Washington, Maryland">\n        Fort Washington\n       </a>\n       . Numerous\n       <a href="/wiki/Indian_Americans" title="Indian Americans">\n        Indian Americans\n       </a>\n       live across the state, especially in central Maryland.\n       <a href="/wiki/Amish" title="Amish">\n        Amish\n       </a>\n       /\n       <a href="/wiki/Mennonite" title="Mennonite">\n        Mennonite\n       </a>\n       communities are found in\n       <a href="/wiki/St._Mary%27s_County,_Maryland" title="St. Mary\'s County, Maryland">\n        St. Mary\'s\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Garrett_County,_Maryland" title="Garrett County, Maryland">\n        Garrett\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Cecil_County,_Maryland" title="Cecil County, Maryland">\n        Cecil\n       </a>\n       counties.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-amishamerica_107-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-amishamerica-107">\n         [107]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Attracting educated Asians and Africans to the professional jobs in the region, Maryland has the fifth-largest proportions of racial minorities in the country.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108">\n        <a href="#cite_note-108">\n         [108]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In 2006 645,744 were counted as foreign born, which represents mainly people from Latin America and Asia. About 4.0 percent are\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Undocumented_immigrants" title="Undocumented immigrants">\n        undocumented immigrants\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-109">\n        <a href="#cite_note-109">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maryland also has a large Korean American population.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110">\n        <a href="#cite_note-110">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In fact, 1.7 percent are Korean, while as a whole, almost 6.0 percent are Asian.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111">\n        <a href="#cite_note-111">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       According to The Williams Institute\'s analysis of the 2010 U.S. Census, 12,538 same-sex couples are living in Maryland, representing 5.8 same-sex couples per 1,000 households.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-freedomtomarry.org_112-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-freedomtomarry.org-112">\n         [112]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       As of 2016,\n       <a href="/wiki/Non-Hispanic_whites" title="Non-Hispanic whites">\n        non-Hispanic white Americans\n       </a>\n       were 51.5% of Maryland\'s population, making Maryland on the verge of becoming a\n       <a href="/wiki/Majority_minority" title="Majority minority">\n        majority minority\n       </a>\n       state. 48.5% of Maryland\'s population is non-white and/or Hispanic/Latino, the highest percentage of any state on the\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States" title="East Coast of the United States">\n        East Coast\n       </a>\n       and the highest percentage after the majority minority states of Hawaii, New Mexico, Texas, California and Nevada.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113">\n        <a href="#cite_note-113">\n         [113]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Non-Hispanic White Americans in Maryland, the majority as of 2016, are expected to become the plurality ethnic group within 5 years of 2015.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114">\n        <a href="#cite_note-114">\n         [114]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After Nevada in 2016, Maryland is projected to be the next state to become majority minority due to growing African-American, Asian and Latino populations. By 2031, minorities are projected to become the majority of voting eligible residents of Maryland.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115">\n        <a href="#cite_note-115">\n         [115]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">\n        Religion\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Religion">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="barbox tright" style="overflow-x: auto;">\n       <div style="border:1px solid silver; font-size:88%; padding:0.4em; width:; background: white;">\n        <table style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">\n         <tr style="background:#ddd">\n          <th colspan="5">\n           Religion in Maryland (2014)\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Pew_Religion_and_Politics_116-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-Pew_Religion_and_Politics-116">\n             [116]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n          </th>\n         </tr>\n         <tr style="font-size:88%; height:4px;">\n          <td style="padding:0 4px;">\n           religion\n          </td>\n          <td style="padding:0 4px; text-align:right;">\n          </td>\n          <td style="width:;">\n          </td>\n          <td style="padding:0 4px; width:1em; text-align:right;">\n           percent\n          </td>\n          <td style="padding:0 4px; text-align:right;">\n          </td>\n         </tr>\n         <tr>\n          <td colspan="2" style="padding-left: 0.4em; padding-right: 0.4em; min-width: 8em;">\n           Protestant\n          </td>\n          <td style="width: 100px; border-left: solid 1px silver; border-right: solid 1px silver;">\n           <div style="background:purple; width:52%; overflow: hidden;">\n           </div>\n          </td>\n          <td colspan="2" style="padding-left: 0.4em; padding-right: 0.4em; text-align: right;">\n           52%\n          </td>\n         </tr>\n         <tr>\n          <td colspan="2" style="padding-left: 0.4em; padding-right: 0.4em; min-width: 8em;">\n           None\n          </td>\n          <td style="width: 100px; border-left: solid 1px silver; border-right: solid 1px silver;">\n           <div style="background:black; width:23%; overflow: hidden;">\n           </div>\n          </td>\n          <td colspan="2" style="padding-left: 0.4em; padding-right: 0.4em; text-align: right;">\n           23%\n          </td>\n         </tr>\n         <tr>\n          <td colspan="2" style="padding-left: 0.4em; padding-right: 0.4em; min-width: 8em;">\n           Catholic\n          </td>\n          <td style="width: 100px; colspan="2" style="padding-left: 0.4em; padding-right: 0.4em; text-align: right;">\n           15%\n          </td>\n         </tr>\n         <tr>\n          <td colspan="2" style="padding-left: 3%\n          </td>\n         </tr>\n         <tr>\n          <td colspan="2" style="padding-left: 0.4em; padding-right: 0.4em; min-width: 8em;">\n           Other faiths\n          </td>\n          <td style="width: 100px; border-left: solid 1px silver; border-right: solid 1px silver;">\n           <div style="background:gray; width:2%; overflow: hidden;">\n           </div>\n          </td>\n          <td colspan="2" style="padding-left: 0.4em; padding-right: 0.4em; text-align: right;">\n           2%\n          </td>\n         </tr>\n         <tr>\n          <td colspan="2"        </td>\n          <td style="width: 100px; border-left: solid 1px silver; border-right: solid 1px silver;">\n           <div style="background:orange; width:1%; overflow: hidden;">\n           </div>\n          </td>\n          <td colspan="2" style="padding-left: 0.4em; padding-right: 0.4em; text-align: right;">\n           1%\n          </td>\n         </tr>\n         <tr>\n          <td colspan="2" style="padding-left: 0.4em; padding-right: 0.4em; min-width: 8em;">\n           Islam\n          </td>\n          <td style="width: 100px; border-left: solid 1px silver; border-right:
